There was Puzhu, Rorschach (didn't like but was different), Nanpakal Nerathu Mayakkam, Kathal - The Core and now this Bramayugam. This is what superstars should do, rather than being pressurized to only deliver blockbusters and do regular masala stuff. If the Superstars get the audience to watch these movies and like some, the audience's taste also improves helping other such movies. Kudos to Mammookka !!!
